href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TOKYO-BOUND/1530739317173813"&gt;TOKYO BOUND&lt;/a&gt; A new monthly dance night starting on December 27th at Squid Ink Sushi Cityscape hosted by KandyK. Myself... &lt;a class="profileLink" href="https://www.facebook.com/djdefensemekanizm"&gt;DJ Defense Mekanizm&lt;/a&gt; will be djing electro &amp; pop music and every month will feature live artists. This month is tattooer Siege and Jay Espinoza of Revival Art Collective. Drink and food specials 10PM-2AM. &lt;br /&gt; ____________________________________________&lt;br /&gt; Leave it to international tattooed icons KandyK and Suzy Homewrecker to bring the fashion-meets-art finesse o&lt;span class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span class="text_exposed_show"&gt;f Haute Harajuku to City Scape in downtown Phoenix, suiting up Squid Ink Sushi with Tokyo-bondage couture, kinky Kawaii chaos, and Japanese high fashion for the aptly titled Tokyo Bound Part fetish fest and part dress-up event, this monthly dance party is the citys answer to Lolita exotica and avant-garde expressionism.&lt;br /&gt; From 10pm to 2am every last Saturday of the month, you are invited to dine on sushi and drink specials while donning your most licentious latex and chic Betsey Johnson apparel. Pick your hors doeuvres right off the flesh of human offerings. Roller derby and dance party queen Suzy Homewrecker is DJ Defense.Mekanizm for the evening, blasting enough electro and pop to get heels clicking and boots stomping. British pin-up darling KandyK is your hostess. Siege and Jay Espinoza of Revival Art Collective are the opening nights visual executors. Expect live artists and photographers galore every month for this pretty-in-punk bash.&lt;br /&gt; Human sushi platters, studded kisses and spikes, and freaky fashion pageantrythe union of these tattooed vixens is the visual kei extravaganza that will light up downtown in ruffles, laces, latex, and sugary sweet fetishista.&lt;br /&gt; - Zander Buel&lt;br /&gt; Opening Night December 27th class="text_exposed_hide"&gt;...&lt;/span&gt;&lt;div class="text_exposed_show"&gt;&lt;p&gt; Arizona Derby Dames Banked Track - Season 10&lt;br /&gt; What better way to take a break between holidays than with a double header roller derby bout!!! We&#039;ve got some exciting match ups that will bring you to the edge of your seats! First we have the Brutal Beauties taking on the Runaway Brides. Second match up will be the Bombshells VS The Schoolyard Scrappers!&lt;br /&gt; Come join us at this fast action event!&lt;br /&gt; The Dames will also be hosting a toy drive. More information on this to come, so keep an eye out!&lt;br /&gt; Bout Day Information&lt;br /&gt; -\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\&lt;br /&gt; The Arizona Derby Dames&#039; Hall of Dames is located at 2517 West McDowell Road, Suite 118, Phoenix, AZ 85009. Fans who have not yet been to the Hall of Dames will find A-Frame signs and parking attendants dressed in safety orange shirts to help direct them to the entrance on the south side of McDowell Road, just west of the I-17 Freeway. As always, parking at the Hall of Dames is free of charge.&lt;br /&gt; Doors will open at 5:00 p.m. with the first whistle at 6:00 p.m. General admission tickets at the door are $20 for adults and $7 for for children 12 and under. Discounted tickets can be purchased in advance for $15 at&lt;br /&gt; Bleacher seating is available on a first come first served basis and for those with disabilities. Additional standing room on raised platforms and track side benches are available as well.&lt;br /&gt; Immediately following the bouts, the Derby Dames will be headed to Steel Horse Saloon for their official Afterparty. Steel Horse Saloon is located at 1818 W Bell Rd in North Phoenix. Due to Arizona statutes, the Afterparty is restricted to fans 21 and older.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt; About the Arizona Derby Dames&lt;br /&gt; -\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\-\&lt;br /&gt; Arizona Derby Dames (AZDD) is an all-women&#039;s banked track roller derby league based in the Phoenix, Arizona metropolitan area. Its foremost priorities are to provide top-notch training, achieve the highest national ranking, set the standard for roller derby leagues worldwide,&lt;br /&gt; and to instill the values of hard work and dedication in AZDD members that lead to success in all aspects of life. AZDD is the the first league to play banked track roller derby in Arizona since the 1960&#039;s and is a founding member of the Roller Derby Coalition of Leagues.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;span
